## üß¨ WHAT ARE **PEPTIDES**?

**Peptides** are **short chains of amino acids**, usually 2‚Äì50 in length. Think of them as **mini proteins** ‚Äî small enough to signal specific functions in your body **without triggering major side effects**.

They are like **biological text messages** your cells send each other to:
- heal tissue ü©π
- grow hair üíá‚Äç‚ôÄÔ∏è
- burn fat üî•
- boost focus üß†
- regenerate nerves ‚ö°
- even improve sexual function üòè

---

## üß† PEPTIDES VS. PROTEINS

| Property       | Peptides                          | Proteins                     |
|----------------|-----------------------------------|------------------------------|
| Size           | Tiny (2‚Äì50 amino acids)           | Big (>50 amino acids)        |
| Function       | Specific signals (e.g., repair)   | Structural (muscles, enzymes)|
| Absorption     | Often injectable or nasal         | Broken down in digestion     |
| Examples       | BPC-157, TB-500, Semax, Selank    | Collagen, Insulin, Hemoglobin|

---

## ‚öôÔ∏è HOW DO THEY WORK?

Peptides bind to receptors on your cells and **tell your body to do something it already knows how to do** ‚Äî like repair a tendon, grow neurons, or regulate stress hormones. They don‚Äôt *force* a foreign effect like a drug; they *remind* your body of a natural signal.

Some examples:
- **Semax** ‚Üí boosts BDNF ‚Üí better focus + cognition  
- **TB-500** ‚Üí activates actin-binding proteins ‚Üí tissue healing

### Why it broke

* The roads shapefile is huge (every curve-point is stored).  
* A KML file has to be a single plaintext XML document; with this many vertices the in-memory string explodes past the parser‚Äôs safety limit and produces a malformed token error.

### Two ways to get the **real, labelled, no-placeholder** overlay on your phone to-night

| Option | What you do | Result |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| **A ‚Äì One-click web converter** (fastest) | 1. Press **Convert** ‚Üí **Download**. | You‚Äôll get one merged KML containing every real road segment + the true park boundary. Import it straight into Google Earth Mobile (*Projects ‚ñ∏ Open ‚ñ∏ Browse*). |
| **B ‚Äì QGIS desktop (most control)** | 1.  Install the free GIS app **QGIS** (Windows/Mac/Linux). <br>2.  `Layer ‚ñ∏ Add Layer ‚ñ∏ Add Vector‚Ä¶` ‚Üí point to the `.shp` files from each ZIP. <br>3. Drag-drop into Google Earth on your phone. |
